Letter of Appreciation

Dear Management of Wyndham Grand Plaza Royale Huayu Chongqing,

I would like to express my heartfelt gratitude to Mr. Guo Xinpeng, the manager at your esteemed hotel. This morning, when I was having breakfast at the hotel's restaurant without a breakfast voucher, Mr. Guo kindly provided us with complimentary breakfast vouchers. Furthermore, he offered us some fruits upon our departure, demonstrating his care and hospitality towards guests.

Mr. Guo Xinpeng not only maintains a neat and professional appearance but also consistently wears a warm smile and provides excellent service. His meticulous attention to detail and friendly demeanor greatly enhanced our stay, making it incredibly comfortable and pleasant. His exemplary service reflects the high standards of management at your hotel and showcases the level of excellence expected from a five-star establishment like Wyndham Grand Plaza Royale Huayu Chongqing.

Therefore, I would like to specifically commend Mr. Guo Xinpeng and thank him for his outstanding service. If I visit Chongqing again for business, I will certainly choose to stay at this hotel.

Sincerely,  
Kai
